<date>1595893773794< /date><Pics>[{'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipNZb0FCDqFw5vnVGoX2zDNz0AAXW5By0L0VNyOW=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipMM8t9ByDJAlXVFIj0TVr2hShf1FTWpJ4g7jmmy=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipMk6iUQGHguImf6cUx0_2N3IhzErhq935tD62yr=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipN2la5viCrbdH00-h-JeMiY-3yTdTOqI64hBHqo=w150-h150-k-no-p']}]< /Pics>< user_name>
Brittany Estrada< /user_name>
<response>None< /response>< text>
A great place for family camping.  Has vault toilets and showers but they were not accessible during our trip.  The campgrounds were very clean and the bathrooms were maintained daily.  Beware if you are a t-mobile customer... you will not have reception here.  Cell reception was lost in Murphy.  A short walk down to the river to dip your feet and some fishing.  The sites are first come, first served and each site is allowed 2 cars.  You can make payment with cash or check.  There is also a camp host onsite which we did not need during our 4 day stay.  Lots of other attractions within 20 minute drive including a small market and gas station about 5 minutes down the hill.<//text>

I been here many many times and it's one of the cheapest camp grounds you can come buy while still having lots to do here. There is a hiking trail and fishing spot. No need for a campfire permit on this ground but still good to have. Great place for family camping. Fills up fast, host was mia, be prepared for restrooms being accidently locked by campers. Close river access decent fishing for small trout. Beautiful river canyon. Plenty of firewood if you look for it. Forest service were really great, had programs for kids. Not the place to avoid people.. all in all a positive expirence. We stayed 5 nights.< /Review>

< Review>
Came here with my friend during our lunch hour. There was no line around 1:30 pm, but there were a decent amount of people inside. I can imagine it gets crowded at this restaurant, as it isn't that big. The prices were fair, especially for downtown sf.

We ordered the chicken karaage to share and each got the hinodeya ramen. The chicken was enough to share between two. It also came with matcha salt, but I don't think it really added to the dish. The chicken was really juicy and tasty alone. The ramen came out shortly after. We loved that it came with an egg, which was super good. The pork was really flavorful as well. The broth was great and the noodles were cooked perfectly. We both finished our bowls clean.

We loved the meal here. Service was great and we can't wait to come back once shelter in place ends.< /Review>

Cons:

2) The meat was slightly concerning as it appeared fatty, but it didn‚Äôt feel fatty when being eaten.

< Text>
This is my second time coming to Hinodeya. Came here for lunch for a table of two, and arrived around 12pm, no wait, but it was pretty busy.

Second time ordering the Spicy Miso Ramen - which is the downtown special. The broth is just right with a kick. Pretty good.

Chicken Kaarage is hot, juicy, and crispy! Yum. The matcha salt is served on the side, didn't taste like anything special to me.

Really, the show stealer for me is the Warabi Mochi!! It's soft, bouncy, but just absolutely melts in your mouth. Absolutely delicious.

Service this time was alright. Not sure if our waitress was distracted, or just couldn't hear right, but basically had to re-confirm our ramen orders (after she had left to put it in), and also brought mochi ice cream when I ordered warabi mochi.

My tip is to come early if you have a larger party, otherwise you may need to wait a bit.<//Text>

<Rate>3< /Rate>< text>
I chose the spicy miso ramen, while not a huge fan of spicy soups, I knew from the other location that they take time to ensure a well made broth, which they did and it did not dissappoint. It appeared to be a Sapporo style medium to heavy style broth great mouth feel from the fattiness with each bite. The noodles were a little on the soft side, I'd prefer them a bit harder. Cashu needs more fat and time to cook was a bit chewy. Ajitsuke was passable if this was Sapporo style then this is acceptable.  The spice did not overwhelm and was able to finish without stopping to sweat. I will say the service could use work, the noodle portion is not very large and I could have used more noodles before my broth was cold but was not able to get a server to do this. Also the fast casual feel is a bit off putting because of the level of quality put in, you would like it to be a bit more orderly and put together but it's simply not.<//text>

<name>Athena Chang</name><time>1561840569453< /time><Rating>4<//Rating><review>We got here at 1130AM so there was no wait at all. The menu was pretty simple and includes appetizers, a select few ramen choices and beverages. I was looking for a spicy ramen option but they didn't have one. Instead, i got the Hinodeya Ramen, that is pork based. My coworkers got the chicken ramen and Zen ramen. The noodles came really fast actually, which was quite surprising. My bowl comes with bamboo shoot, half boiled egg, a few pork slices and some green. The broth was exceptional. Normally, i don't feel satisfied until there is some spice in my bowl of noodles but this broth is just amazing! The ramen noodle itself is also very different. It is chewy and seemed homemade of wheat and other ingredients. Now, the bamboo shoots and boiled egg were also excellent. The pork slices were generous and the flavor is on the lighter side. I personally, think it can be a bit saltier and a little tenderer. But all in all, it is a 5-star bowl of ramen noodles.

What I think the restaurant can improve is to stop checking in on us to get us out of the door! For the less-than-1-hr time we were there, i think they asked 3 or 4 times if we needed dessert, or anything after we clearly finished our noodles. There was a long cue at the door already i assumed but it was a bit rude to keep rushing customers.

I am sure the ramen place is only 2 blocks away from work as this will certainly be one of my favorite spots in winter!< /review><pictures>[{'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipNUBdqKCcRg6f4ofpLlTADJjtUzrvGuBWRxdlPB=w150-h150-k-no-p']}]<//pictures><Response>None< /Response><Gmap_id>0x8085817155606cdb:0xb8b346e6940f517e</Gmap_id></record></dataset><record>

< review>
Portion is good. I ordered the House ramen, there were 3 slices of meat, lot of bamboo, and lot of scallion. The noodle and soup both tasted great.  Pricing at $15-$16 and ended up around $18-$22 after tax and tips. This is a bowl of ramen I felt my money was well spent.

This is an abnormal serving portion comparing other ramen restaurants. In other regular ramen restaurants, I normally see 1 slice of meat and just a sprinkle of toppings.

I absolute love this restaurant and will visit again when I am in San Fran. Can you please open a branch in New York?< /review>

Went to this barbecue place last year but it was closed.  Went back yesterday and picked up a rack of pork ribs.  Also a small side of sweet potatos with walnuts/pecans (I forgot which).

The ribs were outstanding.  The meat was so tender it had me sucking on the bone!  You can tell the quality of barbequed meat by the way it taste without all the sauces and condiments.  These ribs needed no additional sauce or anything to enhance their smoked flavor.  Although I did use a little of the sauce provided on the side, it was tangy and sweet at the same time.  Most importantly,, it doesn't overpower the meat.  A little bit goes a long way.

The sweet potatoes were tasty as well and complimented the ribs very well. The only thing about this dish was that were a bit too many walnuts/pecans for my taste.  Never the less, I will be returning soon to try their brisket and other offerings.<//Review>

Their brisket rivals the best I've had in Kansas City and Memphis. And like most good BBQ restaurants, they WILL run out of items before closing time. This is the best BBQ I have ever had in California. Serious foodie find.

The second you walk in you will smell wood from the stacks of red oak lining the walls which is used to smoke the meats.

The meat was the best Ive had. The meat is so tender. The Beef ribs were like nothing I have ever seen, it was more like a full steak with a bone attached. The baked beans were the best I have had in my entire life.

Recommend:
-Beef Ribs
-Baked Beans
-Brisket Sandwich
-Peach Cobbler

Owner opened recently (mid covid) and was a former food truck operator. Please patronize this place. In Rancho/Fontana the good privately owned places seem to fold, but it honestly blows away any of the corporate BBQ places near by and I want this place to stick around.< /text>

<pictures>None</pictures>< review>
Finally got time to try Jude‚Äôs BBQ. First thing I noticed - wonderful smoke smell inside the place. Second, the owner works the counter, slicing brisket.  Ordered two brisket sandwiches. He asks, ‚ÄúFatty or Lean?‚Äù (never had a bbq place ask that if me before).  I said his choice, so he gave us a bit of both. Toasted buns. You can get them topped with sauce, pickles, slaw or pickled red onions.  We ordered slaw and beans as sides.

Verdict: Yum!  Some of the best brisket i‚Äôve had in a very long time.  No dry spots, not tough, not overly fat, nice crust & smoke ring. Slaw tasted homemade, beans were loaded with meat & flavor. Sauce is nice, not too ketchupy or sweet, but no burn.

Also available were spareribs, pulled pork, sausage and (today) beef short ribs.

Everybody was masked & gloved up. Hand sanitizer is available on a table.

He said they run out early and close when they do, so come early.

Definitely, Definitely will be back!!< /review>

<response>None</response>< text>
My wife and I were searching for lunch one day and decided to try the new Japanese place, Sansai, on a whim. The interior is clean, not too busy, with attractive tables and booths. An open kitchen so you can see that the cooks are being honest with a cold bar behind glass holding the salad options. I must say I was a little confused by the ordering process, but really it's straight forward. I'm just a little dumb.
We ordered a chicken plate and some kind of a sushi roll (I can't remember now to save my life!). Both were excellent and tasted fresh. I was a little concerned about ordering sushi rolls, and not just a plain old California Roll that you can get from a gas station, but with actual sushi fish on it. Luckily it tasted fine and was not tainted or old. I really liked the salad that came with the entree, and the tomato and cucumber salad on the side. Chicken was not fatty or dry. It was great! We spent about $17 for 2 of us to share a lunch, so it's definitely on the pricey side, especially for a place that comes off as a quick-serve restaurant. But the good news is that the food is good so hopefully this place does well and keeps Restaurant Row looking great!</text>

We came in on a Saturday afternoon in a party of 8 friends and family members, the place is very clean and quite, servers are extremely polite and professional. We ordered salmon, tuna, and shrimp shushi, a couples of salad, and a few bowls of spicy and non-spicy ramen, every dish is in excellent quality and we are extremely satisfied, the total cost is very reasonable given the quality and quantity of the food. This place certainly has the highest quality/price ratio of the numerous Asian restaurants I personally visited in recent past. Will definitely come back when found myself in the area again! <text>Want value?  Yes, SanSai!

Want delicious food?  Yes, SanSai!

Want a quick meal?  Yes, SanSai!

Will we, Cobra Kai, beat the Miyagi Dojo at the All-Valley Karate Tournament?  Yes, SanSai!

SanSai is a quick casual Japanese food spot, located in Lakewood's Restaurant Row (aka Candlewood St.) across the mall.  Specials galore, including daily, lunch & Happy Hour.

Spicy miso ramen-
With a cool overcast day & myself feeling a little chilly, I knew a nice bowl of piping hot ramen would be in store for me.  SanSai has tonkatsu & spicy miso as their ramen options.  Spicy miso is my go-to everywhere, so spicy miso it was.  In a large bowl, the steaming soup of happiness was plentiful.  While the ramen could've been a little more al dente for my personal taste, the chewiness was there and the tender slices of pork were succulent and delicious.  The half egg was a bonus, as I know some popular ramen shops charge extra for that.  Upon receiving my order, I asked for chili oil, as I didn't want to use Sriracha because of the preservatives.  A sauce cup of chili oil was quickly brought to me, upon which I dumped the entire contents into my spicy miso, delivering the right amount of heat I desired.  I happily slurped & gulped it down to the very last drop.  For $8+, the spicy miso ramen was good & about on par with dedicated ramen restaurants.

Plentiful seating, with booths, stools & a communal table.  Service was good.  The menu states ramen takes about 10-15 mins, of which I only waited approximately 5 mins or so for mine.  I was the first customer of the day, however.

Parking is in a private lot, shared by Outback Steakhouse and other businesses.

During my meal of ramen & California roll, I enjoyed listening to Sirius satellite radio on the house speakers.  When I was finishing my soup, it happened.  Yes, it happened!  I was Rick Roll'd!

"Never gonna give you up, never gonna let you down.
Never gonna run around, and desert you."

Aye aye, SanSai!  SanSai offers up delicious Japanese food in a casual setting.  I haven't had ramen in a long while, since the LALALA Ramen Pass promo, so SanSai's spicy miso hit the spot.  Add to that the daily, lunch & Happy Hour specials, and SanSai has a new fan.  Quick, convenient & yummy, I highly recommend SanSai!

NOMNOMNOMNOMNOMNOMNOMNOMNOMNOMNOM< /text>< pictures>
None< /pictures>

We ordered a lot of food for our daughter's birthday though their website. It was a busy Saturday evening, so it took a bit longer than the online ordering system said. Which was no problem, I totally understood and was not upset. Then they brought put the order and apologized and gave me an extra item. It was unexpected and very nice. <text>Maybe it was because they were busy tonight. I decided to try it because of the positive reviews, but once was enough. First, because they are currently open only for takeout, I attempted to call in my order,  but they would not answer their phone. Upon arrival, my first impression was the foul odor. The lighting was very  dim and because I used to work in restaurants, I can usually judge that dim lighting with an obnoxious smell is a good indication that things are not being cleaned. After waiting to order, I then had to wait outside for 30 minutes before the food arrived. That would have been ok too, except that nobody likes really overcooked, soggy veggies in a weird-tasting and very watery sauce. Being hungry, I might have even been ok with that, but it all tasted like over-cooked bell peppers. I had requested no bell pepper because it can be overpowering, especially if overcooked. <Text>I was in the area for an appointment when I suddenly started craving Chinese food. Since I was around a bunch of food spots, I decided to swing by and grab food before heading home. A quick Yelp search and I found myself at Dragon's Pond.
It was around 7:30pm on a Monday and I was surprised to see that it was pretty much empty! I was seated and handed a menu right away.
I started off with Chicken Potstickers (free with Yelp check-in). I also ordered the Beef Fried Rice (~$9) and Shrimp with Broccoli (~$15).
The chicken potstickers were a nice appetizer to start with. They were pan-fried and actually super tasty! It went well with the soy sauce and vinegar sauce on the side. The shrimp with broccoli was a bit too greasy for me but I must say the portion of shrimp and broccoli was pretty fair considering it was a ~$15 dish. The beef fried rice was a bit mediocre; it was lacking salt and basic flavoring on the beef.
Although it didn't quite hit the spot like I hoped, it did last me 3 meals total, which made spending ~$25 a bit more reasonable. It was a good try but I don't think I'd return.<//Text><user_name>Aya Eano< /user_name></record>

<name>Mik Hamilton< /name><time>1535401930959</time><rating>5< /rating>< text>
I'm what's known as a foodie (fickle, obsessive, over-analytical diner), especially when it comes to Chinese food. There are so many types that the words "Chinese food" can't even be relied upon. I would say that Dragon's Pond serves pretty typical Mandarin style dishes with some Asian fusion dishes thrown in for good measure. The room is clean and neat and very modern looking with nice lighting and acoustics. We ordered 5 or 6 dishes, none in which I could find a flaw. (not too oily, not to salty, not to anything). I would order every dish again. The staff were friendly and helpful, to a person. Can't wait to go back.</text>

<Resp>None</Resp><Date>1341788097128< /Date>< review>
I am a regular here and I think this is one of the best Chinese restaurants around. Everything is so fresh and is not like standard Chinese restaurants. Many of the non-traditional dishes are fantastic. The service is top-notch, friendly and full of suggestions and explainations. Some of my favorites are the Hunan Lamb, Seafood Curry, Black Bean Sauce Chow Fun, Elite Eggplant, Eastern-Style Egg Fu Young w/seafood or combination etc. The sauces in the dishes are really well crafted, especially the non-standard sauce for the Egg Fu Young which is exquisite. If you want the best Chinese in Walnut Creek, Dragons Pond is it!</review>

<username>J J<//username><pics>None< /pics>< Review>
Waffles are not bad. Ours were a little on the dry side. The waffles were not light and airy like  I usually expect from Belgian waffles. They were more cakey. Some of the flavor combinations were pretty good. If you like those fruit tarts, the custard and berries was good. Not sure why they do the seating arrangement they do (fast food style). You walk in and order, then find a seat. Seating isn't ample and if you get there when it is busy, people take a seat before they even order. So you may get your food and not have a place to sit and eat it. Not really food you eat on the go and since it is food mainly for one specific mealtime rush, I didn't think that worked very well. We got a seat but the poor group of 5 behind us ended up taking turns sitting and eating at a table for 2. A little chaotic. I was not impressed with the wait staff. Twice I had to call them back to clean up spilled sticky messes (which they kept missing) and finally, had to get some water and a napkin and clean it up myself. Going back to the food, overall, not bad but a little overpriced - sit down restaurant prices for fast food atmosphere. The kids proportion was not worth it. Regular size portion is 2 waffles.  Kids portion is less than 1 waffle. I do think it is worth a try if they are not busy but not someplace I see myself becoming a regular of.</Review>

< Text>
First, let me be clear I am not looking for gourmet or extraordinary tacos and burrito . I just want good, tasty at a decent price. This food was none of those things. First the place is small and does not have many tables ( not a big problem ) but we ordered and waited at least 40 minutes for our food. We ordered tacos, burritos and nachos. The tacos are street tacos very small, flavor was barely ok, burrito was tolerable but the worst was the nachos . How can you charge $7 for a handful of chips and sprinkle of meat and no cheese?! The cheese is velveeta melted cheese and it was so skimpy!! Also their water cups are so small, you'll need at least 4 to make a cup. I'm sorry but it's an embarrassment to be selling this food. I dont recommend it.<//Text>
